### Post by mirrreia on 2015-09-17
Im very new in Ubuntu.
I have installed Ubuntu Studio in a Toshiba Satellite A200-1FL , and old one.
When i installed, all ok, at home i have wifi and is connected.
BUT, in another place, another wifi.....i really have not the option or i dont see it to connect to other wifi.
I read lots of forums, they are all different.
I isntalled Wifi-Radar, but donnow how to connect form it.
Sorry my ignorance, im less than a week new into linux.
is there any way to do it?
my Network Manager app also doesnt let me any option to choose the wifi.
PLEASE HELP.
i love Ubuntu thogh

thanks!

### Post by slickymaster on 2015-09-17

### Post by Bucky Ball on 2015-09-17
Welcome. Slickymaster beat me to it. :)

This is tricky because when you're out and it's not working you can't report back what's happening. You don't need to add any software so I'd uninstall Wifi-Radar. Any available networks anywhere will show up fine with Network Manager just like your home network does (and probably a few neighbours' networks, too). 

Please be specific about the other place and other network. What network are you trying to connect to? University? Open access? Friend's house? If you connect fine at home I'd say the reason you can't connect 'there' is generated by 'there'. :)

You could try changing the 'infrastructure' setting to 'ad-hoc' when you're there by clicking the network icon> Edit> Wireless> Edit> Wifi tab, but I don't think that has anything to do with it. Although it might! Depending on what you're attempting to connect to.

---
